<h1 _ngcontent-sms-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="@ohos.security.huks (通用密钥库系统)"> @ohos.security.huks (通用密钥库系统) </h1>

<div _ngcontent-sms-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>向应用提供密钥库能力，包括密钥管理及密钥的密码学操作等功能。</p>    <p>HUKS所管理的密钥可以由应用导入或者由应用调用HUKS接口生成。</p>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <p>本模块首批接口从API version 8开始支持。后续版本的新增接口，采用上角标单独标记接口的起始版本。</p>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 247px;">     <h2 id="导入模块" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,lite_wearable,tv">导入模块<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="导入模块" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span><span class="support-device-item">Lite Wearable</span></div><div _ngcontent-sms-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-sms-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-sms-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-sms-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,lite_wearable,tv">huks.generateKeyItem<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="huksgeneratekeyitem9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span><span class="support-device-item">Lite Wearable</span></div><p>generateKeyItem(keyAlias: string, options: HuksOptions, callback: AsyncCallback&lt;void&gt;) : void</p>     <p>生成密钥，使用Callback回调异步返回结果。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Security.Huks.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">keyAlias</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">别名。密钥别名的最大长度为128字节，建议不包含个人信息等敏感词汇。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-huks#huksoptions">HuksOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">用于存放生成key所需TAG。其中密钥使用的算法、密钥用途、密钥长度为必选参数。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AsyncCallback&lt;void&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">回调函数。未捕获error时代表用户指定别名的密钥生成成功，基于密钥不出TEE原则，此接口不会返回密钥材料内容，若捕获error，则为生成阶段出现异常。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-huks">HUKS错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.10.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" Possible causes: 1. Mandatory parameters are left unspecified. 2. Incorrect parameter types. 3. Parameter verification failed.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">801</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">api is not supported.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">12000001</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">algorithm mode is not supported.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td communication failed.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">12000006</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">error occurred in crypto engine.</td> style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 2645px;">     <h2 id="huksgeneratekeyitem9-1" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">huks.generateKeyItem<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="huksgeneratekeyitem9-1" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>generateKeyItem(keyAlias: string, options: HuksOptions) : Promise&lt;void&gt;</p>     <p>生成密钥，使用Promise方式异步返回结果。基于密钥不出TEE原则，通过promise不会返回密钥材料内容，只用于表示此次调用是否成功。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Security.Huks.Extension</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">keyAlias</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">密钥别名。密钥别名的最大长度为128字节，建议不包含个人信息等敏感词汇。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-huks#huksoptions">HuksOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">用于存放生成key所需TAG。其中密钥使用的算法、密钥用途、密钥长度为必选参数。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise&lt;void&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise对象。无返回结果的Promise对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>和<a            <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.11.12.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" <p>用于删除时指定密钥的属性TAG，如使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-huks#huksauthstoragelevel11">HuksAuthStorageLevel</a>指定需删除密钥的安全级别，</p>          <p>可传空，当API version ≥ 12时，传空默认为CE，当API version ＜ 12时，传空默认为DE。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table width="50%">Promise对象。无返回结果的Promise对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a id="huksattestkeyitem9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">huks.attestKeyItem<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i width="50%">Promise对象。当调用成功时，HuksReturnResult的certChains成员非空，为获取到的证书链。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a     <h2 id="huksanonattestkeyitem11" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">huks.anonAttestKeyItem<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="huksanonattestkeyitem11" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>anonAttestKeyItem(keyAlias: string, options: HuksOptions, callback: AsyncCallback&lt;HuksReturnResult&gt;) : void</p>     <p>获取匿名化密钥证书，使用Callback方式回调异步返回结果。</p>     <p>该操作需要联网进行，且耗时较长。返回12000012错误码时，可能是由于网络异常导致。此时如果没有联网，需要提示用户网络没有连接，如果已经联网，可能是由于网络抖动导致失败，建议重试。</p>     <p>密钥证明证书格式说明请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/device-attestation-servers#section8815174119330" target="_blank">设备证书服务-密钥证明证书格式说明</a>。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Security.Huks.Extension</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">keyAlias</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">密钥别名，存放待获取证书密钥的别名。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-huks#huksoptions">HuksOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">用于获取证书时指定所需参数与数据。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AsyncCallback&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-huks#huksreturnresult9">HuksReturnResult</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">回调函数。不返回err值时表示接口使用成功，其他时为错误。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-huks">HUKS错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.12.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.12.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">401</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Parameter error. Possible causes: 1. Mandatory parameters are left unspecified. 2. Incorrect parameter types. 3. Parameter verification failed.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">801</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">api is not supported.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">12000001</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">algorithm mode is not supported.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">12000004</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">operating file failed.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 3697px;">     <h2 id="huksanonattestkeyitem11-1" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">huks.anonAttestKeyItem<sup>11+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="huksanonattestkeyitem11-1" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>anonAttestKeyItem(keyAlias: string, options: HuksOptions) : Promise&lt;HuksReturnResult&gt;</p>     <p>获取匿名化密钥证书，使用Promise方式异步返回结果。</p>     <p>该操作需要联网进行，且耗时较长。返回12000012错误码时，可能是由于网络异常导致。此时如果没有联网，需要提示用户网络没有连接，如果已经联网，可能是由于网络抖动导致失败，建议重试。</p>     <p>密钥证明证书格式说明请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/device-attestation-servers#section8815174119330" target="_blank">设备证书服务-密钥证明证书格式说明</a>。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Security.Huks.Extension</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.9.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.9.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.9.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.9.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">keyAlias</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">密钥别名，存放待获取证书密钥的别名。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-huks#huksoptions">HuksOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">用于获取证书时指定所需参数与数据。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.19.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-huks#huksreturnresult9">HuksReturnResult</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise对象。当调用成功时，HuksReturnResult的certChains成员非空，为获取到的证书链。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-huks">HUKS错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> id="huksimportwrappedkeyitem9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,lite_wearable,tv">huks.importWrappedKeyItem<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="huksimportwrappedkeyitem9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span><span class="support-device-item">Lite Wearable</span></div><p>importWrappedKeyItem(keyAlias: string, wrappingKeyAlias: string, options: HuksOptions, callback: AsyncCallback&lt;void&gt;) : void</p>     <p>导入加密密钥，使用Callback方式回调异步返回结果。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Security.Huks.Core</p>     <p>API version 9-11系统能力为SystemCapability.Security.Huks.Extension；从API version 12开始为SystemCapability.Security.Huks.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.20.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">keyAlias</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">密钥别名，存放待导入密钥的别名。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">wrappingKeyAlias</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">密钥别名，对应密钥用于解密加密的密钥数据。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-huks#huksoptions">HuksOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">用于导入时所需TAG和需要导入的加密的密钥数据。其中密钥使用的算法、密钥用途、密钥长度为必选参数。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">回调函数。不返回err值时表示接口使用成功，其他时为错误。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-huks">HUKS错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t"> </li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">/* 以下操作不需要调用HUKS接口，此处不给出具体实现。</span></li><li><span class="hljs-comment">   * 假设待导入的密钥为keyA</span></li><li><span class="hljs-comment">   * 1.生成ECC公私钥keyB，公钥为keyB_pub, 私钥为keyB_pri</span></li><li><span class="hljs-comment">   * 2.使用keyB_pri和wrappingAlias密钥中获取的公钥进行密钥协商，协商出共享密钥share_key</span></li><li><span class="hljs-comment">   * 3.随机生成密钥kek，用于加密keyA，采用AES-GCM加密，加密过程中需要记录：nonce1、aad1、加密后的密文keyA_enc、加密后的tag1。</span></li><li><span class="hljs-comment">   * 4.使用share_key加密kek，采用AES-GCM加密，加密过程中需要记录：nonce2、aad2、加密后的密文kek_enc、加密后的tag2。</span></li><li><span class="hljs-comment">   * 5.拼接importOptions.inData字段，满足以下格式:</span></li><li><span class="hljs-comment">   * keyB_pub的长度（4字节） + keyB_pub的数据 + aad2的长度（4字节） + aad2的数据 +</span></li><li><span class="hljs-comment">   * nonce2的长度（4字节）   + nonce2的数据   + tag2的长度（4字节） + tag2的数据 +</span></li><li><span class="hljs-comment">   * kek_enc的长度（4字节）  + kek_enc的数据  + aad1的长度（4字节） + aad1的数据 +</span></li><li><span class="hljs-comment">   * nonce1的长度（4字节）   + nonce1的数据   + tag1的长度（4字节） + tag1的数据 +</span></li><li><span class="hljs-comment">   * keyA长度占用的内存长度（4字节）  + keyA的长度     + keyA_enc的长度（4字节） + keyA_enc的数据</span></li><li><span class="hljs-comment">   */</span></li><li>  <span class="hljs-comment">/* 该处为示例代码，实际运行过程中，应使用实际导入密钥数据。数据构造方式由上注释可见说明 */</span></li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">let</span> inputKey = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Uint8Array</span>([<span class="hljs-number">0x02</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0x00</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0x00</span>, <span class="hljs-number">0x00</span>]);</li><li>  importOptions.<span class="hljs-property">inData</span> = inputKey;</li><li>  <span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">TestImportWrappedFunc</span>(alias, wrappingAlias, importOptions);</li><li>}</li><li>

device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">huks.importWrappedKeyItem<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="huksimportwrappedkeyitem9-1" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>importWrappedKeyItem(keyAlias: string, wrappingKeyAlias: string, options: HuksOptions) : Promise&lt;void&gt;</p>     <p>导入加密密钥，使用Promise方式异步返回结果。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Security.Huks.Extension</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">keyAlias</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">密钥别名，存放待导入密钥的别名。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">wrappingKeyAlias</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">密钥别名，对应密钥用于解密加密的密钥数据。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-huks#huksoptions">HuksOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">用于导入时所需TAG和需要导入的加密的密钥数据。其中密钥使用的算法、密钥用途、密钥长度为必选参数。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise&lt;void&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise对象。无返回结果的Promise对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>和<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-huks">HUKS错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.12.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.21.12.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">401</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Parameter error. Possible causes: 1. Mandatory parameters are left unspecified. 2. Incorrect parameter types. 3. Parameter verification failed.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">801</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">api is not supported.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">12000001</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">algorithm mode is not supported.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-huks#huksunwrapkeyitem20">unwrapKeyItem</a>对应，待导出的密钥在生成时要添加<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-huks#hukstag">HUKS_TAG_IS_ALLOWED_WRAP</a>，指定密钥允许导出）。使用Promise异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Security.Huks.Core</p> width="25%">密钥别名，应与所用密钥生成时使用的别名相同。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">params</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a width="25%">用于指定导出密钥时的加密类型。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table width="50%">Promise对象。当调用成功时，HuksReturnResult的outData成员非空，为导出的密钥密文。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a    <h2 id="huksgetkeyitemproperties9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,lite_wearable,tv">huks.getKeyItemProperties<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="huksgetkeyitemproperties9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span><span class="support-device-item">Lite Wearable</span></div><p>getKeyItemProperties(keyAlias: string, options: HuksOptions, callback: AsyncCallback&lt;HuksReturnResult&gt;) : void</p>     <p>获取密钥属性，使用Callback回调异步返回结果。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Security.Huks.Core</p>     <p>API version 9-11系统能力为SystemCapability.Security.Huks.Extension；从API version 12开始为SystemCapability.Security.Huks.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">keyAlias</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">密钥别名，应与所用密钥生成时使用的别名相同。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-huks#huksreturnresult9">HuksReturnResult</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">回调函数。不返回err值时表示接口使用成功，其他时为错误。properties：返回值为生成密钥时所需参数。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a            <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.26.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" void</p>     <p>判断密钥是否存在，使用callback异步回调。</p>     <p>若密钥不存在，则通过callback返回false。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong>  </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1559px;">     <h2 id="huksinitsession9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,lite_wearable,tv">huks.initSession<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="huksinitsession9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span><span class="support-device-item">Lite Wearable</span></div><p>initSession(keyAlias: string, options: HuksOptions, callback: AsyncCallback&lt;HuksSessionHandle&gt;) : void</p>     <p>initSession操作密钥接口，使用Callback回调异步返回结果。huks.initSession, huks.updateSession, huks.finishSession为三段式接口，需要一起使用。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Security.Huks.Core</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.32.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.32.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.32.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.32.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">keyAlias</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">initSession操作密钥的别名。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-huks#huksoptions">HuksOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">initSession操作的参数集合。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AsyncCallback&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-huks#hukssessionhandle9">HuksSessionHandle</a>&gt;</td>         <td  <p>表示签名类型为携带认证信息。生成或导入密钥时指定该字段，则在使用密钥进行签名时，对待签名的数据添加认证信息后进行签名。</p>          <p><strong>注意：</strong></p>          <p>携带的认证信息包含身份信息，开发者需在其隐私声明中对此身份信息的使用目的、存留策略和销毁方式进行说明。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 543px;">     <h2 id="huksauthstoragelevel11"   <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 997px;">     <h2 id="huksgetsdkversiondeprecated" class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getSdkVersion(options: HuksOptions) : string</p>     <p>获取当前系统sdk版本。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">huks.generateKey<sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="huksgeneratekeydeprecated" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>generateKey(keyAlias: string, options: HuksOptions, callback: AsyncCallback&lt;HuksResult&gt;) : void</p>     <p>生成密钥，使用Callback回调异步返回结果。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 9开始废弃，建议使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-huks#huksgeneratekeyitem9">huks.generateKeyItem<sup>9+</sup></a>替代。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.Security.Huks.Extension</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.68.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.68.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.68.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.68.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">keyAlias</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">别名。密钥别名的最大长度为128字节，建议不包含个人信息等敏感词汇。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">options</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-huks#huksoptions">HuksOptions</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">用于存放生成key所需TAG。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AsyncCallback&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-huks#huksresultdeprecated">HuksResult</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>abort(handle: number, options: HuksOptions, callback: AsyncCallback&lt;HuksResult&gt;) : void</p>     <p>abort操作密钥接口，使用Callback回调异步返回结果。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 9开始废弃，建议使用<a class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 9开始废弃，建议使用<a
